All Ages until midnight\r\n\r\nWith an existing roster that includes recent and forthcoming releases by The Amity Affliction, The Getaway Plan, Deez Nuts, Dream On Dreamer, House Vs Hurricane, I Killed The Prom Queen and more recently The Bride UNFD is proud to announce the newest addition to their already booming roster that encompasses the cream of the crop of Australian heavy music, and welcome young up-and-coming act from the Western Sydney hardcore scene, Northlane to the family!\r\n\r\nFor a long time, we didnt sign any new bands as we felt there was a bit of a talent vacuum, and we pride ourselves in only releasing music we find original and inspiring to us personally. says A&R Manager, Luke Logemann. Now, the quality of music coming out of the Sydney hardcore and metal scenes is simple too good to ignore. Northlane epitomises everything that this new breed of Australian hardcore is about  progressive song writing, a powerful live show, and especially, a strong message.\r\n\r\nNorthlane have spent the last 2 years touring constantly around Australia, building up fanbases in regional and city centres without the use of supports or marketing behind them. Their strong focus on technical musicianship and live performance has attracted fans of all walks of life, and garnered the attention of multiple labels. But for the band, UNFD was always where they wanted to be.\r\n\r\nSigning to UNFD has been almost surreal for us, says Guitarist Josh Smith. There arent many labels in Australia signing bands like us, but UNFD are carving a market of their own and going from strength to strength. Their track record is impeccable and its humbling to be on a roster with such amazing bands. We worked so hard, for so long and were picked over for other bands and knocked back on countless occasions. We never let that dissuade us from what we love doing, we kept our heads up and luckily someone recognised that. Were looking forward to the future with great anticipation and were so excited about finally being able to give this album to our supporters whove waited so long for it. Thanks UNFD, you guys rule!\r\n\r\nTheir debut album, Discoveries was produced by the band themselves, and mixed in New Jersey by Will Putney at Machineshop  the same studio UNFD worked with on The Amity Afflictions Youngbloods album. And the results contain the same heavy-yet-melodic energy that the studio is famous for.\r\n\r\nUNFD will release Discoveries on a short turn around of just a month  unleashing the monster of a debut on 11.11.11 (November 11, 2011). Fans can hear the first track from the album Dispossession now on UNFDs YouTube Channel and Blog. To get an mp3 version, sign up to the bands mailing list link below.\r\n\r\nJoining the show are local favourites Admella for the launch of their debut EP that has seen months of work gone into development and production.
